```bash
python3 - <<'PY'
import sqlite3
po='/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_sjeng_bpdb_off_5m/bp.db'
pn='/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_sjeng_bpdb_on_5m/bp.db'

def load(path):
    con=sqlite3.connect(path)
    con.execute('pragma temp_store=2')
    b={}
    for pc,rows,mis in con.execute('select branchPC,count(*),sum(predTaken!=actualTaken) from tagemisstrace group by branchPC'):
        b[pc]={'rows':rows,'mis':mis or 0}
    mt={}
    for pc,t,c in con.execute('select branchPC,mainTable,count(*) from tagemisstrace where mainFound=1 group by branchPC,mainTable'):
        mt.setdefault(pc,{})[t]=c
    ua={}
    for pc,c in con.execute('select branchPC,sum(useAlt=1) from tagemisstrace group by branchPC'):
        ua[pc]=c or 0
    con.close()
    return b,mt,ua

bo,mto,uao=load(po)
bn,mtn,uan=load(pn)
allpcs=set(bo)|set(bn)
rows=[]
for pc in allpcs:
    o=bo.get(pc,{'rows':0,'mis':0}); n=bn.get(pc,{'rows':0,'mis':0})
    orows,om=o['rows'],o['mis']; nrows,nm=n['rows'],n['mis']
    if min(orows,nrows)<200:
        continue
    orate=om/orows if orows else 0
    nrate=nm/nrows if nrows else 0
    dmis=nm-om
    drate=nrate-orate
    omt=mto.get(pc,{})
    nmt=mtn.get(pc,{})
    os=sum(t*c for t,c in omt.items()); oc=sum(omt.values())
    ns=sum(t*c for t,c in nmt.items()); nc=sum(nmt.values())
    oavg=os/oc if oc else -1
    navg=ns/nc if nc else -1
    duse=((uan.get(pc,0)/nrows if nrows else 0) - (uao.get(pc,0)/orows if orows else 0))
    rows.append((dmis,drate,pc,orows,nrows,om,nm,orate,nrate,oavg,navg,duse))
rows.sort(key=lambda x:(x[0],x[1]),reverse=True)
print('TOP_WORSEN')
for r in rows[:30]:
    dmis,dr,pc,orows,nrows,om,nm,orate,nrate,oavg,navg,duse=r
    if dmis<=0: break
    print(f"0x{pc:x} {dmis:+d} {dr:+.4f} {orows}->{nrows} {om}->{nm} rate {orate:.4f}->{nrate:.4f} avgTbl {oavg:.2f}->{navg:.2f} dUseAlt {duse:+.4f}")
rows.sort(key=lambda x:(x[0],x[1]))
print('TOP_IMPROVE')
for r in rows[:30]:
    dmis,dr,pc,orows,nrows,om,nm,orate,nrate,oavg,navg,duse=r
    if dmis>=0: break
    print(f"0x{pc:x} {dmis:+d} {dr:+.4f} {orows}->{nrows} {om}->{nm} rate {orate:.4f}->{nrate:.4f} avgTbl {oavg:.2f}->{navg:.2f} dUseAlt {duse:+.4f}")
PY
```

```bash
import sqlite3
for name,p in [('gobmk_off','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_gobmk_bpdb_off_5m/bp.db'),('gobmk_on','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_gobmk_bpdb_on_5m/bp.db'),('sjeng_off','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_sjeng_bpdb_off_5m/bp.db'),('sjeng_on','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_sjeng_bpdb_on_5m/bp.db')]:
    con=sqlite3.connect(p)
    con.execute('pragma temp_store=2')
    total=con.execute('select sum(predTaken!=actualTaken) from tagemisstrace').fetchone()[0]
    q='''with s as (select startPC from tagemisstrace group by 1 having count(distinct branchPC)>=2)
         select count(*),sum(predTaken!=actualTaken) from tagemisstrace t join s using(startPC)'''
    rows,mis=con.execute(q).fetchone()
    con.close()
    print(name,'rows',rows,'misp',mis,'misp_pct',round(mis/total*100,2))
PY
```

```bash
import sqlite3

def table_rates(path):
    con=sqlite3.connect(path)
    d={t:(rows,mis) for t,rows,mis in con.execute('select mainTable,count(*),sum(predTaken!=actualTaken) from tagemisstrace where mainFound=1 group by mainTable')}
    con.close();return d
for bench,off,on in [
('gobmk','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_gobmk_bpdb_off_5m/bp.db','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_gobmk_bpdb_on_5m/bp.db'),
('sjeng','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_sjeng_bpdb_off_5m/bp.db','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_sjeng_bpdb_on_5m/bp.db')]:
    do=table_rates(off); dn=table_rates(on)
    print('===',bench)
    for t in sorted(set(do)|set(dn)):
        orows,omis=do.get(t,(0,0)); nrows,nmis=dn.get(t,(0,0))
        orate=omis/orows if orows else 0
        nrate=nmis/nrows if nrows else 0
        print(t,orows,nrows,round((nrows-orows)/orows*100,2) if orows else 0,round(orate*100,2),round(nrate*100,2),round((nrate-orate)*100,2))
```

## Assistant (16:41)

**你的判断是对的：需要更细归因，`allocFailure` 下降本身不是坏事。**

我已经把 `gobmk/sjeng` 的 `off/on + bp.db` 做了同口径对比，结论是：

1. **确实存在你说的同 fetch block 多分支冲突**，而且大多在 32B/64B 内。  
2. **但这版替换策略变差的主因，不是这类冲突本身**，而是“全局分配行为变形”，导致更多分支进入低质量预测路径。  
3. **低表分配确实偏激进了**，这个方向还有很大调参空间。

---

**为什么说“全局污染/不该替换”发生了（有证据）**

基于 `bp.db`：

1. `gobmk`（off -> on）  
- 总误判：`37081 -> 38024`（`+943`）  
- `mainFoundRate`：`88.21% -> 86.02%`（下降）  
- `altFoundRate`：`59.58% -> 53.98%`（明显下降）  
- `useAltRate`：`16.21% -> 18.86%`（上升）  
- `main counter` 平均置信度：`5.67 -> 5.52`（下降）  
- `alt counter` 平均置信度：`4.09 -> 3.78`（下降）

2. `sjeng`（off -> on）  
- 总误判：`40747 -> 40988`（`+241`）  
- `mainFoundRate`：`90.85% -> 90.55%`（下降）  
- `altFoundRate`：`63.11% -> 60.88%`（下降）  
- `useAltRate`：`13.31% -> 14.12%`（上升）  
- 置信度也有下降趋势。

这组信号很一致：  
**你把“分配成功”提上去了，但把“可用主预测/可用备选预测”的稳定性拉低了。** 这就是“全局污染”的具体表现。

---

**是不是低表太积极？是的，证据很强**

`mainTable` 分布变化（off -> on）：

1. `gobmk`  
- `t0` provider 行数 `+7.65%`  
- `t1/t3/t6` provider 行数明显下降  
- `t1/t2/t3/t6` 的误判率都上升

2. `sjeng`  
- `t0` provider 行数 `+6.97%`  
- `t2/t3/t4/t5/t6` provider 行数下降  
- `t2/t3/t5/t6` 误判率上升明显

`allocSuccess` 按表也有同方向变化：  
`table0/1/2` 分配增多，`table3/4` 分配减少。  
这说明当前 score-victim 在低表触发太频繁，改变了 provider 生态。

---

**那“同 block 冲突”到底占多大？**

`mainTable+mainIndex` 冲突导致的误判占比（当前 position-mix 基线下）：

1. `gobmk`：`661 / 37081 = 1.78%`  
2. `sjeng`：`608 / 40747 = 1.49%`

所以它是“真实问题”，但不是这次退化的主导项。  
你提到的热点块确实能看到，比如 `gobmk 0x4f384/0x4f572`、`sjeng 0x291a0/0x21b80` 这些都在 trace 里很明显。

---

**你问“分配策略还有没有空间？”有，而且很大**

建议优先做这三条（从最稳妥到激进）：

1. **把 score-victim 限到更低表**  
- `allocScoreMaxTable: 3 -> 1` 先试  
- 目标：减少对中高表稳定条目的扰动

2. **收紧替换阈值**  
- `allocScoreReplaceThreshold: 10 -> 6/4`  
- 让“被替换候选”更弱才允许替换

3. **增加保护条件**  
- 仅当 `mainFound=0` 且 `altFound=0` 时允许 score-victim  
- 或仅在同一 set 持续 alloc fail 达到阈值后才触发（节流）

---

**关于你说的 warmup/run 分离**

你这个担心非常合理。  
现在是 `5M` 直跑，确实可能把“学习期扰动”混进最终结论。  
建议下一步做一组统一口径：

1. `warmup 5M + run 5M`（只看 run stats）  
2. 比较 `off / on / on-收紧阈值 / on-maxTable=1`  
3. 同时导出 bp.db，只看 run 窗口

---

如果你同意，我下一步直接做两件事：  
1. 先改成“保守版 score-victim（maxTable=1 + 低阈值 + 触发节流）”并本地跑 `gobmk/sjeng 5M`。  
2. 再加一组 trace 字段（记录每次 score-victim 的 victim `useful/counter/table`），把“到底替掉了谁”做成可量化报表。

## User (16:43)

## Assistant (16:52)

[Tool: exec_command]

```bash
python3 - <<'PY'
from pathlib import Path
cases={
'gobmk_base':'/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_gobmk_off_5m/stats.txt',
'gobmk_aggr':'/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_gobmk_on_5m/stats.txt',
'gobmk_c1':'/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_c1_gobmk_5m/stats.txt',
'sjeng_base':'/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_sjeng_off_5m/stats.txt',
'sjeng_aggr':'/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_sjeng_on_5m/stats.txt',
'sjeng_c1':'/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_c1_sjeng_5m/stats.txt',
}
keys=['system.cpu.ipc','system.cpu.commit.branchMispredicts','system.cpu.branchPred.tage.condPredwrong','system.cpu.branchPred.tage.updateAllocSuccess','system.cpu.branchPred.tage.updateAllocFailure','system.cpu.branchPred.tage.updateUseAlt','system.cpu.branchPred.tage.updateUseAltWrong']
for n,p in cases.items():
    txt=Path(p).read_text().splitlines()
    d={}
    for ln in txt:
        for k in keys:
            if ln.startswith(k+' '):
                d[k]=float(ln.split()[1])
    ua=d['system.cpu.branchPred.tage.updateUseAlt']
    print(n,d['system.cpu.ipc'],int(d['system.cpu.commit.branchMispredicts']),int(d['system.cpu.branchPred.tage.updateAllocSuccess']),int(d['system.cpu.branchPred.tage.updateAllocFailure']),f"useAltWrongRate={d['system.cpu.branchPred.tage.updateUseAltWrong']/ua:.4f}")
PY
```

```bash
from pathlib import Path
cases=[
('base','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_gobmk_off_5m/stats.txt'),
('aggr','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_gobmk_on_5m/stats.txt'),
('c2','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_c2_gobmk_5m/stats.txt'),

('c4','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_c4_gobmk_5m/stats.txt'),
]

    lines=Path(p).read_text().splitlines();d={}

    ua=d['system.cpu.branchPred.tage.updateUseAlt']
```

## Assistant (17:01)

我接下来做精细归因：对“表现最好的两组”开 `bp.db`，直接统计 `allocByScore` 触发频次、victim 是否 useful、victim 置信度分布，以及这些触发与误判的关系。先并行跑：`gobmk-c3` 和 `sjeng-c2`。

## Assistant (17:01)

## Assistant (17:04)

[Tool: exec_command]

```bash
python3 - <<'PY'
import sqlite3
from collections import defaultdict

def metrics(name, db, base_db):
    con=sqlite3.connect(db); con.execute('pragma temp_store=2')
    c=con.cursor()
    total=c.execute('select count(*) from tagemisstrace').fetchone()[0]
    mis=c.execute('select sum(predTaken!=actualTaken) from tagemisstrace').fetchone()[0]
    alloc_succ=c.execute('select sum(allocSuccess=1) from tagemisstrace').fetchone()[0]
    alloc_score=c.execute('select sum(allocByScore=1) from tagemisstrace').fetchone()[0]
    alloc_score_useful=c.execute('select sum(allocByScore=1 and allocVictimUseful=1) from tagemisstrace').fetchone()[0]
    alloc_score_nonuseful=c.execute('select sum(allocByScore=1 and allocVictimUseful=0) from tagemisstrace').fetchone()[0]
    print(f'=== {name}')
    print('total',total,'mis',mis,'allocSuccess',alloc_succ,'allocByScore',alloc_score,'scoreShare',round(alloc_score/max(alloc_succ,1)*100,2),'%')
    if alloc_score:
        print('scoreVictim useful/nonUseful',alloc_score_useful,alloc_score_nonuseful,'usefulRate',round(alloc_score_useful/alloc_score*100,2),'%')
        r=c.execute('select avg(allocVictimConf), avg(allocVictimScore) from tagemisstrace where allocByScore=1').fetchone()
        print('scoreVictim avgConf/avgScore',round(r[0],3),round(r[1],3))
        print('score alloc by table:')
        for t,n in c.execute('select allocTable,count(*) from tagemisstrace where allocByScore=1 group by allocTable order by allocTable'):
            print(' t',t,n)
        print('score victim conf hist:')
        for conf,n in c.execute('select allocVictimConf,count(*) from tagemisstrace where allocByScore=1 group by allocVictimConf order by allocVictimConf'):
            print(' conf',conf,n)
    # mispredict delta by branch vs baseline
    bcur=sqlite3.connect(base_db).cursor()
    base={pc:mis for pc,mis in bcur.execute('select branchPC,sum(predTaken!=actualTaken) from tagemisstrace group by branchPC')}
    curr={pc:mis for pc,mis in c.execute('select branchPC,sum(predTaken!=actualTaken) from tagemisstrace group by branchPC')}
    deltas=[]
    allpcs=set(base)|set(curr)
    for pc in allpcs:
        d=(curr.get(pc,0) or 0)-(base.get(pc,0) or 0)
        deltas.append((d,pc,base.get(pc,0) or 0,curr.get(pc,0) or 0))
    deltas.sort(reverse=True)
    print('top worsen with score-alloc counts:')
    for d,pc,bm,cm in deltas[:12]:
        if d<=0: break
        sa=c.execute('select count(*) from tagemisstrace where allocByScore=1 and branchPC=?',(pc,)).fetchone()[0]
        print(f' 0x{pc:x} d={d:+d} base={bm} cur={cm} scoreAlloc={sa}')
    deltas.sort()
    print('top improve with score-alloc counts:')
    for d,pc,bm,cm in deltas[:12]:
        if d>=0: break
        sa=c.execute('select count(*) from tagemisstrace where allocByScore=1 and branchPC=?',(pc,)).fetchone()[0]
        print(f' 0x{pc:x} d={d:+d} base={bm} cur={cm} scoreAlloc={sa}')
    con.close()

metrics(
 'gobmk_c3_vs_base',
 '/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_c3_gobmk_bpdb_5m/bp.db',
 '/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_gobmk_bpdb_off_5m/bp.db'
)
metrics(
 'sjeng_c2_vs_base',
 '/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_c2_sjeng_bpdb_5m/bp.db',
 '/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_sjeng_bpdb_off_5m/bp.db'
)
PY
```

```bash
export SQLITE_TMPDIR=/tmp; python3 - <<'PY'
import sqlite3
curr='/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_c3_gobmk_bpdb_5m/bp.db'
base='/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_gobmk_bpdb_off_5m/bp.db'
con=sqlite3.connect(curr); con.execute('pragma temp_store=2'); c=con.cursor()
print('rows/mis',c.execute('select count(*),sum(predTaken!=actualTaken) from tagemisstrace').fetchone())
print('allocSuccess/allocByScore',c.execute('select sum(allocSuccess=1),sum(allocByScore=1) from tagemisstrace').fetchone())
print('score useful/nonUseful',c.execute('select sum(allocByScore=1 and allocVictimUseful=1),sum(allocByScore=1 and allocVictimUseful=0) from tagemisstrace').fetchone())
print('score by table',list(c.execute('select allocTable,count(*) from tagemisstrace where allocByScore=1 group by allocTable order by allocTable')))
print('score conf hist',list(c.execute('select allocVictimConf,count(*) from tagemisstrace where allocByScore=1 group by allocVictimConf order by allocVictimConf')))
print('score top branches',list(c.execute('select printf("0x%x",branchPC),count(*) c from tagemisstrace where allocByScore=1 group by branchPC order by c desc limit 15')))
# branch deltas
bcon=sqlite3.connect(base); bcon.execute('pragma temp_store=2'); b=bcon.cursor()
base_m={pc:(m or 0) for pc,m in b.execute('select branchPC,sum(predTaken!=actualTaken) from tagemisstrace group by branchPC')}
cur_m={pc:(m or 0) for pc,m in c.execute('select branchPC,sum(predTaken!=actualTaken) from tagemisstrace group by branchPC')}
d=[]
for pc in set(base_m)|set(cur_m):
    dv=cur_m.get(pc,0)-base_m.get(pc,0)
    d.append((dv,pc,base_m.get(pc,0),cur_m.get(pc,0)))
d.sort(reverse=True)
print('top worsen')
for dv,pc,bm,cm in d[:20]:
    if dv<=0: break
    sa=c.execute('select count(*) from tagemisstrace where allocByScore=1 and branchPC=?',(pc,)).fetchone()[0]
    print(hex(pc),dv,bm,cm,sa)
d.sort()
print('top improve')
for dv,pc,bm,cm in d[:20]:
    if dv>=0: break
    sa=c.execute('select count(*) from tagemisstrace where allocByScore=1 and branchPC=?',(pc,)).fetchone()[0]
    print(hex(pc),dv,bm,cm,sa)
con.close(); bcon.close()
PY
```

## Assistant (17:05)

[Tool: exec_command]

```bash
python3 - <<'PY'
import sqlite3
pairs=[
('gobmk_base','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_gobmk_bpdb_off_5m/bp.db'),
('gobmk_c3','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_c3_gobmk_bpdb_5m/bp.db'),
('sjeng_base','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_sjeng_bpdb_off_5m/bp.db'),
('sjeng_c2','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_c2_sjeng_bpdb_5m/bp.db')
]
for n,p in pairs:
    con=sqlite3.connect(p);con.execute('pragma temp_store=2');c=con.cursor()
    total,mis=c.execute('select count(*),sum(predTaken!=actualTaken) from tagemisstrace').fetchone()
    mainf,altf,usealt=c.execute('select sum(mainFound=1),sum(altFound=1),sum(useAlt=1) from tagemisstrace').fetchone()
    mnot,mnotmis=c.execute('select sum(mainFound=0),sum(mainFound=0 and predTaken!=actualTaken) from tagemisstrace').fetchone()
    mUse, mMain = c.execute('select sum(predTaken!=actualTaken and useAlt=1),sum(predTaken!=actualTaken and useAlt=0) from tagemisstrace').fetchone()
    am,aa=c.execute('select avg(abs(mainCounter*2+1)),avg(abs(altCounter*2+1)) from tagemisstrace').fetchone()
    print(n,'mis',mis,'mainFound%',round(mainf/total*100,2),'altFound%',round(altf/total*100,2),'useAlt%',round(usealt/total*100,2),'mainNotFoundRows',mnot,'mainNotFoundMisp',mnotmis,'misUseAlt',mUse,'misMainOnly',mMain,'avgConfMain/Alt',round(am,3),round(aa,3))
    con.close()
PY
```

## Assistant (17:05)

[Tool: exec_command]

```bash
python3 - <<'PY'
import sqlite3
for n,p in [('gobmk_base','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_gobmk_bpdb_off_5m/bp.db'),('gobmk_c3','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_c3_gobmk_bpdb_5m/bp.db'),('sjeng_base','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_sjeng_bpdb_off_5m/bp.db'),('sjeng_c2','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_c2_sjeng_bpdb_5m/bp.db')]:
    con=sqlite3.connect(p);con.execute('pragma temp_store=2');c=con.cursor()
    q='''WITH base AS (SELECT * FROM TAGEMISSTRACE),
idx_alias AS (SELECT startPC, mainTable, mainIndex FROM base WHERE mainFound=1 GROUP BY 1,2,3 HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT branchPC)>=2),
way_alias AS (SELECT startPC, mainTable, mainIndex, wayIdx FROM base WHERE mainFound=1 GROUP BY 1,2,3,4 HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT branchPC)>=2)
SELECT (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM base),
       (SELECT SUM(predTaken!=actualTaken) FROM base),
       (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM base b JOIN idx_alias a USING(startPC,mainTable,mainIndex)),
       (SELECT SUM(b.predTaken!=b.actualTaken) FROM base b JOIN idx_alias a USING(startPC,mainTable,mainIndex)),
       (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM base b JOIN way_alias a USING(startPC,mainTable,mainIndex,wayIdx)),
       (SELECT SUM(b.predTaken!=b.actualTaken) FROM base b JOIN way_alias a USING(startPC,mainTable,mainIndex,wayIdx));'''
    total,mis,ir,im,wr,wm=c.execute(q).fetchone()
    print(n,'idx_alias_mis%',round(im/mis*100,2),'way_alias_mis%',round(wm/mis*100,2),'idx_rows',ir,'way_rows',wr)
    con.close()
PY
```

## Assistant (17:09)

[Tool: exec_command]

```bash
python3 - <<'PY'
from pathlib import Path
files=[('base','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_wm5r5_base_gobmk/stats.txt'),('c3','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_wm5r5_c3_gobmk/stats.txt')]
keys=['simInsts','system.cpu.ipc','system.cpu.commit.branchMispredicts','system.cpu.branchPred.tage.condPredwrong','system.cpu.branchPred.tage.updateAllocSuccess','system.cpu.branchPred.tage.updateAllocFailure']
for name,p in files:
    lines=Path(p).read_text().splitlines()
    # split into blocks by begin marker
    begins=[i for i,l in enumerate(lines) if l.startswith('---------- Begin Simulation Statistics')]
    blocks=[]
    for bi,b in enumerate(begins):
        e=begins[bi+1] if bi+1<len(begins) else len(lines)
        blocks.append(lines[b:e])
    print('===',name,'blocks',len(blocks))
    for idx,blk in enumerate(blocks):
        d={}
        for ln in blk:
            for k in keys:
                if ln.startswith(k+' '): d[k]=ln.split()[1]
        print(' block',idx,{k:d.get(k,'NA') for k in keys})
PY
```

```bash
python3 - <<'PY'
from pathlib import Path
files=[('base','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_wm5r5_base_sjeng/stats.txt'),('c2','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_wm5r5_c2_sjeng/stats.txt')]
keys=['simInsts','system.cpu.ipc','system.cpu.commit.branchMispredicts','system.cpu.branchPred.tage.condPredwrong','system.cpu.branchPred.tage.updateAllocSuccess','system.cpu.branchPred.tage.updateAllocFailure']
for name,p in files:
    lines=Path(p).read_text().splitlines()
    begins=[i for i,l in enumerate(lines) if l.startswith('---------- Begin Simulation Statistics')]
    print('===',name,'blocks',len(begins))
    for bi,b in enumerate(begins):
        e=begins[bi+1] if bi+1<len(begins) else len(lines)
        blk=lines[b:e]
        d={}
        for ln in blk:
            for k in keys:
                if ln.startswith(k+' '): d[k]=ln.split()[1]
        print(' block',bi,{k:d.get(k,'NA') for k in keys})
PY
```

## Assistant (17:14)

[Tool: exec_command]

```bash
python3 - <<'PY'
import sqlite3
cases=[
('gobmk','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_c3_gobmk_bpdb_5m/bp.db','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_gobmk_bpdb_off_5m/bp.db'),
('sjeng','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_c2_sjeng_bpdb_5m/bp.db','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_sjeng_bpdb_off_5m/bp.db')
]
for name,curr,base in cases:
    cc=sqlite3.connect(curr).cursor(); bb=sqlite3.connect(base).cursor()
    touched={pc for (pc,) in cc.execute('select distinct branchPC from tagemisstrace where allocByScore=1')}
    cur={pc:(m or 0) for pc,m in cc.execute('select branchPC,sum(predTaken!=actualTaken) from tagemisstrace group by branchPC')}
    bas={pc:(m or 0) for pc,m in bb.execute('select branchPC,sum(predTaken!=actualTaken) from tagemisstrace group by branchPC')}
    dt=0; du=0; nt=0; nu=0
    for pc in set(cur)|set(bas):
        d=cur.get(pc,0)-bas.get(pc,0)
        if pc in touched:
            dt+=d; nt+=1
        else:
            du+=d; nu+=1
    print(name,'touched_branches',len(touched),'delta_on_touched',dt,'delta_on_untouched',du,'total',dt+du)
PY
```

```bash
export SQLITE_TMPDIR=/tmp; python3 - <<'PY'
import sqlite3
for name,curr,base in [
('gobmk','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_c3_gobmk_bpdb_5m/bp.db','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_gobmk_bpdb_off_5m/bp.db'),
('sjeng','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_c2_sjeng_bpdb_5m/bp.db','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_sjeng_bpdb_off_5m/bp.db')]:
    conc=sqlite3.connect(curr); conc.execute('pragma temp_store=2'); cc=conc.cursor()
    conb=sqlite3.connect(base); conb.execute('pragma temp_store=2'); bb=conb.cursor()
    touched={pc for (pc,) in cc.execute('select distinct branchPC from tagemisstrace where allocByScore=1')}
    cur={pc:(m or 0) for pc,m in cc.execute('select branchPC,sum(predTaken!=actualTaken) from tagemisstrace group by branchPC')}
    bas={pc:(m or 0) for pc,m in bb.execute('select branchPC,sum(predTaken!=actualTaken) from tagemisstrace group by branchPC')}
    dt=du=0
    for pc in set(cur)|set(bas):
        d=cur.get(pc,0)-bas.get(pc,0)
        if pc in touched: dt+=d
        else: du+=d
    print(name,'touched',len(touched),'delta_touched',dt,'delta_untouched',du,'total',dt+du)
    conc.close(); conb.close()
PY
```

```bash
python3 - <<'PY'
from pathlib import Path
pairs=[
('gobmk','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_wm5r5_base_gobmk/stats.txt','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_wm5r5_c3_gobmk/stats.txt','c3'),
('sjeng','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_wm5r5_base_sjeng/stats.txt','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_wm5r5_c2_sjeng/stats.txt','c2'),
]
keys=['system.cpu.ipc','system.cpu.commit.branchMispredicts','system.cpu.branchPred.tage.condPredwrong','system.cpu.branchPred.tage.updateAllocFailure','system.cpu.branchPred.tage.updateAllocSuccess']

def read_last_block(path):
    lines=Path(path).read_text().splitlines()
    begins=[i for i,l in enumerate(lines) if l.startswith('---------- Begin Simulation Statistics')]
    b=begins[-1]
    blk=lines[b:]
    d={}
    for ln in blk:
        for k in keys:
            if ln.startswith(k+' '):d[k]=float(ln.split()[1])
    return d
for bench,bp,cp,cname in pairs:
    b=read_last_block(bp); c=read_last_block(cp)
    print('===',bench,'run-phase last block',cname,'vs base')
    for k in keys:
        dv=(c[k]/b[k]-1)*100
        print(k,int(b[k]) if b[k].is_integer() else round(b[k],6),'->',int(c[k]) if c[k].is_integer() else round(c[k],6),f'({dv:+.3f}%)')
PY
```

## Assistant (15:17)

[Tool: exec_command]

```bash
export SQLITE_TMPDIR=/tmp; python3 - <<'PY'
import sqlite3
cases=[
('gobmk_c3','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_c3_gobmk_bpdb_5m/bp.db','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_gobmk_bpdb_off_5m/bp.db'),
('sjeng_c2','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_c2_sjeng_bpdb_5m/bp.db','/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv2_sjeng_bpdb_off_5m/bp.db')
]
for name,curr,base in cases:
    con=sqlite3.connect(curr); con.execute('pragma temp_store=2'); c=con.cursor()
    bcon=sqlite3.connect(base); bcon.execute('pragma temp_store=2'); b=bcon.cursor()
    score_rows=c.execute('select count(*) from tagemisstrace where allocByScore=1').fetchone()[0]
    score_starts=c.execute('select count(distinct startPC) from tagemisstrace where allocByScore=1').fetchone()[0]
    score_in_multistart=c.execute('''with s as (select startPC from tagemisstrace group by 1 having count(distinct branchPC)>=2)
                                  select count(*) from tagemisstrace t join s using(startPC) where allocByScore=1''').fetchone()[0]
    print('===',name,'score_rows',score_rows,'distinct_startPC',score_starts,'in_multibranch_startPC',score_in_multistart, f'({score_in_multistart/max(score_rows,1)*100:.2f}%)')
    print('top score startPC: startPC scoreRows scoreMisp branchSet')
    q='''select startPC,count(*) as scoreRows,sum(predTaken!=actualTaken) as scoreMisp,
                (select group_concat(distinct printf('0x%x',branchPC)) from tagemisstrace t2 where t2.startPC=t1.startPC and t2.allocByScore=1) as bset
         from tagemisstrace t1 where allocByScore=1
         group by startPC order by scoreRows desc limit 12'''
    for sp,rows,mis,bset in c.execute(q):
        print(hex(sp),rows,mis,bset)
    # startPC-level mis delta on score startPCs
    base_m={sp:(m or 0) for sp,m in b.execute('select startPC,sum(predTaken!=actualTaken) from tagemisstrace group by startPC')}
    cur_m={sp:(m or 0) for sp,m in c.execute('select startPC,sum(predTaken!=actualTaken) from tagemisstrace group by startPC')}
    score_s={sp for (sp,) in c.execute('select distinct startPC from tagemisstrace where allocByScore=1')}
    delta_score=sum(cur_m.get(sp,0)-base_m.get(sp,0) for sp in score_s)
    delta_non=sum(cur_m.get(sp,0)-base_m.get(sp,0) for sp in set(cur_m)|set(base_m) if sp not in score_s)
    print('misp delta on score-startPC',delta_score,'non-score-startPC',delta_non,'total',delta_score+delta_non)
    con.close(); bcon.close()
PY
```

- 新增保守参数与门限：
  - [src/cpu/pred/BranchPredictor.py](/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/src/cpu/pred/BranchPredictor.py)

---

**5M直跑结果（你当前常用口径）**

gobmk（基线 vs 各配置）：
- `base`: IPC `2.583373`, mispred `42686`, allocFail `6121`

- `base`: IPC `2.129908`, mispred `47429`, allocFail `7263`

- `c2`: IPC `-0.165%`, mispred `-0.310%`, allocFail `-5.74%`
- `c3`: IPC `-0.868%`, mispred `+0.649%`, allocFail `-17.49%`

对应目录示例：
- [gobmk c3 5m](/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_c3_gobmk_5m/stats.txt)

- [sjeng warmup/run base](/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_wm5r5_base_sjeng/stats.txt)
- [sjeng warmup/run c2](/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_wm5r5_c2_sjeng/stats.txt)

---

**trace细化归因（新字段）**

`bp.db`：
- [gobmk c3 bpdb](/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_c3_gobmk_bpdb_5m/bp.db)
- [sjeng c2 bpdb](/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/debug/tage_replv3_c2_sjeng_bpdb_5m/bp.db)

gobmk c3：
- `allocByScore = 774`，占 `allocSuccess` 的 `2.61%`
- 全部替换 `non-useful` victim（符合 `allowUseful=F`）
- 主要在 `table1`（`610` 次）和 `table0`（`164` 次）
- 约 `70.5%` 发生在“多分支 startPC”块
- mispred 总体相对 base：`-206`（5M口径）

sjeng c2：
- `allocByScore = 72`，占 `allocSuccess` 的 `0.22%`
- `71` 次 non-useful，`1` 次 useful
- 主要在 `table0`
- 约 `68.1%` 发生在多分支块
- mispred 总体相对 base：`-117`（5M口径）

**解释**
- 这说明 score-victim 的确在你关心的“密集多分支块”触发了。  
- 但在更稳定的 warmup+run 口径，收益没保住，说明它更像“前期缓解冲突/训练加速”，不是“长期稳态改进”。

---

**结论与建议（落地）**
1. 现在不建议直接把当前 score-victim 配置上 CI 作为主方案。  
2. 下一步应做“阶段化策略”：仅 warmup 阶段开 score-victim，run 阶段自动关闭。  
3. 或者做“自适应门控”：根据近期 `mainFound/altFound` 和 mispred 滑窗动态开关，不要常开。  

如果你同意，我下一步直接实现“**warmup-only score-victim**”开关，并复跑同样两组 `wm5r5`，看是否能保留 allocFailure 下降且不伤 run-phase 准确率。

## Assistant (15:37)

**结论先说**
你这个目标我理解为：`2-way / 小容量` 下，通过算法把效果拉近 `4-way`。  
就我这轮数据看，**目前还做不到“稳定达到 4-way 效果”**。  
更准确地说：`5M直跑` 有局部收益，但到 `warmup+run` 稳态阶段收益会消失甚至反转。

---

**这次方案到底做了什么**

我做了两层改动：

1. **替换算法加“可控保守化”开关**  
在 [BranchPredictor.py](/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/src/cpu/pred/BranchPredictor.py)、[btb_tage.hh](/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/src/cpu/pred/btb/btb_tage.hh)、[btb_tage.cc](/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/src/cpu/pred/btb/btb_tage.cc) 增加了：
- `allocScoreRequireBothMiss`
- `allocScorePressureThreshold`
- `allocScoreAllowUsefulVictim`

你可以把它理解成三道闸门：
- 是否只在 main/alt 都 miss 才触发
- 是否达到一定“压力”才触发
- 是否允许替换 useful 条目

2. **trace 增强，能直接归因“替了谁”**  
在 [common.hh](/nfs/home/yanyue/workspace/GEM5_review/src/cpu/pred/btb/common.hh) 给 `TAGEMISSTRACE` 加了：
- `allocByScore`
- `allocVictimUseful`
- `allocVictimConf`
- `allocVictimTaken`
- `allocVictimScore`

这样不是只看 `allocFailure`，而是能看到“score替换触发频次、替换对象质量、在哪些表触发”。

---

**效果怎么样（核心结果）**

**A. 5M 直跑（你当前快速筛选口径）**

- `gobmk` 最好的是 `c3`：  
  - mispred: `42686 -> 42630`（小幅好）  
  - allocFailure: `6121 -> 4765`（明显降）  
  - IPC: `2.583373 -> 2.580461`（略降）

- `sjeng` 最好的是 `c2`：  
  - mispred: `47429 -> 47282`（小幅好）  
  - allocFailure: `7263 -> 6846`（小幅降）  
  - IPC: `2.129908 -> 2.126400`（略降）

**B. warmup 5M + run 5M（更接近稳态）**

- `gobmk`（base vs c3，run段）  
  - mispred: `38614 -> 38937`（变差）  
  - IPC: `2.829572 -> 2.820425`（变差）  
  - allocFailure: `24163 -> 23165`（仍下降）

- `sjeng`（base vs c2，run段）  
  - mispred: `40479 -> 40596`（变差）  
  - IPC: `2.277649 -> 2.278443`（几乎持平）  
  - allocFailure: `20311 -> 20236`（微降）

这说明：  
**它确实减少了分配失败，但没有稳定转化成 run-phase 预测收益。**

---

**你问“尽量小容量达到4ways效果，目前是不是不行？”**

我的判断：**按“统一参数 + 稳态run段”标准，目前不行。**

补充一点你会关心的：
- 你历史 `ways4` 结果里，`gobmk_b1` 的 mispred 是 `42224`，明显优于 base `42686`。  
- 我这轮最好的 `c3` 只有 `42630`，离 `42224` 还差一截。  
- 所以在 gobmk 上，“小容量 + 替换算法”暂时没达到你想要的 `4-way` 提升幅度。

---

**为什么会这样（归因）**

从增强后的 trace 看：

- `gobmk c3` 的 `allocByScore` 有 `774` 次（占 alloc success `2.61%`），主要在 table0/1。  
- `sjeng c2` 的 `allocByScore` 只有 `72` 次（占 `0.22%`）。  
- 触发位置约 `70%` 在你说的“同 fetch block 多分支”场景，方向是对的。  
- 但 run-phase 结果表明它更像“局部解堵”，没有形成长期稳定收益。

也就是：  
**我们把“分配失败”问题处理了，但还没把“长期正确保留关键条目”处理好。**

---

如果你同意，我下一步就做你更需要的版本：  
`warmup-only score-victim`（只在 warmup 开，run 自动关），然后按同样 `wm5r5` 口径复测。  
这个更符合你“尽量小容量拿到接近4-way收益”的工程路径。
